import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import api from '../../utils/api.js';
import { Trash2, Building2 } from 'lucide-react';

export default function CompanyList({ companies, onRefresh }) {
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);

  const handleDeleteCompany = async (companyId, companyName) => {
    if (!window.confirm(`Báº¡n cÃ³ cháº¯c cháº¯n muá»‘n xÃ³a cÃ´ng ty "${companyName}"? HÃ nh Ä‘á»™ng nÃ y khÃ´ng thá»ƒ hoÃ n tÃ¡c!`)) {
      return;
    }

    setLoading(true);
    try {
      await api.delete(`/api/companies/${companyId}`);
      alert('ÄÃ£ xÃ³a cÃ´ng ty thÃ nh cÃ´ng!');
      onRefresh();
    } catch (err) {
      alert(err.response?.data?.error || 'Lá»—i xÃ³a cÃ´ng ty!');
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };

  if (!companies || companies.length === 0) {
    return (
      <div className="bg-white p-5 rounded-2xl border border-slate-200 shadow-sm">
        <h3 className="text-xs font-bold text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider flex items-center gap-1.5 mb-4">
          <Building2 size={16} className="text-blue-600" /> Danh sÃ¡ch cÃ´ng ty / PhÃ¡p nhÃ¢n
        </h3>
        <p className="text-sm text-slate-500 text-center py-6">ChÆ°a cÃ³ cÃ´ng ty nÃ o. Vui lÃ²ng thÃªm cÃ´ng ty má»›i bÃªn trÃªn.</p>
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className="bg-white p-5 rounded-2xl border border-slate-200 shadow-sm space-y-4">
      <h3 className="text-xs font-bold text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider flex items-center gap-1.5">
        <Building2 size={16} className="text-blue-600" /> Danh sÃ¡ch cÃ´ng ty / PhÃ¡p nhÃ¢n
      </h3>
      <div className="overflow-x-auto">
        <table className="w-full text-left border-collapse text-xs">
          <thead>
            <tr className="bg-slate-50 border-b border-slate-200 font-bold text-slate-600">
              <th className="p-3">TÃªn cÃ´ng ty</th>
              <th className="p-3">MÃ£ sá»‘ thuáº¿</th>
              <th className="p-3">Äá»‹a chá»‰</th>
              <th className="p-3 text-center">HÃ nh Ä‘á»™ng</th>
            </tr>
          </thead>
          <tbody className="divide-y divide-slate-100">
            {companies.map(company => (
              <tr key={company.id} className="hover:bg-slate-50/50 transition">
                <td className="p-3 font-bold text-slate-700">{company.name}</td>
                <td className="p-3 text-slate-600">{company.tax_code}</td>
                <td className="p-3 text-slate-600">{company.address || '--'}</td>
                <td className="p-3 text-center">
                  <button
                    onClick={() => handleDeleteCompany(company.id, company.name)}
                    disabled={loading}
                    className="p-1.5 text-slate-400 hover:text-rose-600 rounded-xl hover:bg-rose-50 transition disabled:opacity-50 disabled:cursor-not-allowed"
                    title="XÃ³a cÃ´ng ty"
                  >
                    <Trash2 size={15} />
                  </button>
                </td>
              </tr>
            ))}
          </tbody>
        </table>
      </div>

  );
}



=== FILE: front-end\src\views\admin\CompanyManagement.jsx ===

import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import api from '../../utils/api.js';
import { useAuth } from '../../context/AuthContext.jsx';
import AddCompanyForm from './AddCompanyForm.jsx';
import CompanyList from './CompanyList.jsx';
import { ShieldAlert, Users, UserPlus, Trash2, KeyRound } from 'lucide-react';

export default function CompanyManagement() {
  // Láº¥y danh sÃ¡ch dá»¯ liá»‡u vÃ  hÃ m load tá»« Context chung cá»§a há»‡ thá»‘ng
  const { fetchCompanies, companies, user: currentUser, loadUsers } = useAuth();

  const [localUsers, setLocalUsers] = useState([]);
  const [loadingUsers, setLoadingUsers] = useState(true);

  const syncLocalUsers = (userList) => {
    setLocalUsers(Array.isArray(userList) ? userList.map(user => ({
      ...user,
      company_id: Array.isArray(user.company_ids) ? (user.company_ids[0] || null) : null
    })) : []);
  };

  // Use centralized loader from AuthContext to avoid divergent user state
  const fetchUsersFromApi = async () => {
    try {
      const data = await loadUsers();
      return Array.isArray(data) ? data : [];
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Lá»—i táº£i danh sÃ¡ch nhÃ¢n sá»± tá»« Context:', err);
      return [];
    }
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    const init = async () => {
      setLoadingUsers(true);
      const [companiesList, usersList] = await Promise.all([
        fetchCompanies().catch((err) => {
          console.error('Lá»—i táº£i danh sÃ¡ch cÃ´ng ty:', err);
          return [];
        }),
        fetchUsersFromApi()
      ]);
      syncLocalUsers(usersList);
      setLoadingUsers(false);
    };

    init();
  }, [fetchCompanies]);

  // States quáº£n lÃ½ Form thÃªm nhÃ¢n viÃªn má»›i
  const [newUsername, setNewUsername] = useState('');
  const [newPassword, setNewPassword] = useState('');
  const [newRole, setNewRole] = useState('nv');
  const [newManagerId, setNewManagerId] = useState('');
  const [newCompanyIds, setNewCompanyIds] = useState([]);

  const toggleCompanySelection = (companyId) => {
    setNewCompanyIds(prev => {
      if (prev.includes(companyId)) {
        return prev.filter(id => id !== companyId);
      }
      return [...prev, companyId];
    });
  };

  // Thay Ä‘á»•i Ä‘Æ¡n vá»‹ cÃ´ng tÃ¡c trá»±c tiáº¿p trÃªn báº£ng
  const handleAssign = async (userId, companyId) => {
    const targetCompanyId = companyId ? Number(companyId) : null;
    const targetUser = localUsers.find(u => u.id === userId);

    if (targetUser?.username === 'admin') {
      alert('KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ cáº¥u hÃ¬nh Ä‘Æ¡n vá»‹ cÃ´ng tÃ¡c cho tÃ i khoáº£n Root!');
      return;
    }

    setLocalUsers(prev => prev.map(u =>
      u.id === userId ? { ...u, company_id: targetCompanyId } : u
    ));

    try {
      await api.post('/api/auth/assign-company', {
        userId,
        companyId: targetCompanyId,
        companyIds: targetCompanyId ? [targetCompanyId] : [],
        role: targetUser?.role || 'nv'
      });
      const updatedUsers = await fetchUsersFromApi();
      syncLocalUsers(updatedUsers);
    } catch (err) {
      alert('Lá»—i gÃ¡n quyá»n Ä‘Æ¡n vá»‹');
      const updatedUsers = await fetchUsersFromApi();
      syncLocalUsers(updatedUsers);
    }
  };

  // Thay Ä‘á»•i Vai trÃ² trá»±c tiáº¿p trÃªn báº£ng
  const handleRoleChange = async (userId, newRole) => {
    const targetUser = localUsers.find(u => u.id === userId);

    if (targetUser?.username === 'admin') {
      alert('Cáº¥m tuyá»‡t Ä‘á»‘i hÃ nh vi tÆ°Æ¡ng tÃ¡c hoáº·c thay Ä‘á»•i vai trÃ² cá»§a tÃ i khoáº£n Root há»‡ thá»‘ng!');
      return;
    }

    if (userId === currentUser?.id) {
      alert('Báº¡n khÃ´ng thá»ƒ tá»± thay Ä‘á»•i vai trÃ² cá»§a chÃ­nh mÃ¬nh!');
      return;
    }

    setLocalUsers(prev => prev.map(u =>
      u.id === userId ? {
        ...u,
        role: newRole,
        company_id: newRole === 'admin' ? null : u.company_id
      } : u
    ));

    try {
      await api.post('/api/auth/assign-company', {
        userId,
        companyId: newRole === 'admin' ? null : (targetUser?.company_id || null),
        companyIds: newRole === 'admin' ? [] : (targetUser?.company_id ? [targetUser.company_id] : []),
        role: newRole
      });
      const updatedUsers = await fetchUsersFromApi();
      syncLocalUsers(updatedUsers);
    } catch (err) {
      alert('Lá»—i cáº­p nháº­t vai trÃ²');
      const updatedUsers = await fetchUsersFromApi();
      syncLocalUsers(updatedUsers);
    }
  };

  const handleAddUser = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    if (!newUsername || !newPassword) {
      alert('Vui lÃ²ng nháº­p tÃ i khoáº£n vÃ  máº­t kháº©u!');
      return;
    }
    try {
      const companyIdsPayload = newRole === 'admin' ? [] : newCompanyIds.map(Number).filter(id => id > 0);
      const res = await api.post('/api/users', {
        username: newUsername,
        password: newPassword,
        role: newRole,
        companyIds: companyIdsPayload,
        managerId: newRole === 'nv' ? (newManagerId ? Number(newManagerId) : null) : null
      });

      const createdUser = res.data?.user;

        setLocalUsers(prev => [
          ...prev,
          {
            ...createdUser,
            company_ids: companyIdsPayload,
            company_id: companyIdsPayload[0] || null,
            manager_id: newRole === 'nv' ? (newManagerId ? Number(newManagerId) : null) : null
          }
        ]);
      }

      alert('ThÃªm nhÃ¢n sá»± má»›i thÃ nh cÃ´ng!');
      setNewUsername('');
      setNewPassword('');
      setNewCompanyIds([]);
      setNewManagerId('');
      setNewRole('nv');
      
      const refreshedUsers = await fetchUsersFromApi();
      syncLocalUsers(refreshedUsers);
    } catch (err) {
      alert(err.response?.data?.error || 'Lá»—i thÃªm nhÃ¢n sá»± má»›i!');
    }
  };

  const handleDeleteUser = async (userId, username) => {

      alert('TÃ i khoáº£n Root há»‡ thá»‘ng lÃ  báº¥t tá»­, khÃ´ng thá»ƒ xÃ³a!');

    }
    if (userId === currentUser?.id) {
      alert('Báº¡n khÃ´ng thá»ƒ tá»± xÃ³a tÃ i khoáº£n cá»§a chÃ­nh mÃ¬nh!');
      return;
    }
    if (!window.confirm(`Báº¡n cÃ³ cháº¯c cháº¯n muá»‘n xÃ³a tÃ i khoáº£n "${username}" khá»i há»‡ thá»‘ng?`)) return;

      alert('ÄÃ£ xÃ³a nhÃ¢n sá»± thÃ nh cÃ´ng!');
      const refreshedUsers = await fetchUsersFromApi();
      syncLocalUsers(refreshedUsers);
    } catch (err) {
      alert(err.response?.data?.error || 'Lá»—i xÃ³a nhÃ¢n sá»±!');
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      <div className="border-b border-slate-200 pb-4">
        <h1 className="text-xl font-black text-slate-800 flex items-center gap-2">

        </h1>

            </h3>
            
            <form onSubmit={handleAddUser} className="space-y-3">

                  value={newUsername}

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { useAuth } from '../../context/AuthContext.jsx';
import { usePersistentState } from '../../utils/persistence.js';

export default function ChangePassword() {
  const { changePassword } = useAuth();
  const [form, setForm] = usePersistentState('change-password-form', { oldPassword: '', newPassword: '', confirm: '' });
  const [error, setError] = useState('');
  const [success, setSuccess] = useState(false);

  const handleSubmit = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setError('');
    if (form.newPassword !== form.confirm) return setError('Máº­t kháº©u má»›i khÃ´ng khá»›p');
    try {
      await changePassword(form.oldPassword, form.newPassword);
      setSuccess(true);
    } catch (err) { setError(err); }
  };

  if (success) return (
    <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-slate-50 p-4">
      <div className="w-full max-w-md bg-white p-6 rounded-2xl shadow text-center">
        <h2 className="text-lg font-black text-emerald-600">Äá»•i máº­t kháº©u thÃ nh cÃ´ng</h2>
        <p className="text-sm text-slate-600 mt-2">Vui lÃ²ng Ä‘Äƒng nháº­p láº¡i náº¿u cáº§n.</p>
        <button onClick={() => location.reload()} className="mt-4 bg-emerald-600 text-white py-2 px-4 rounded">Äá»“ng Ã½</button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-slate-50 p-4">
      <div className="w-full max-w-md bg-white p-6 rounded-2xl shadow space-y-4">
        <h2 className="text-base font-black text-slate-800">Thay Ä‘á»•i máº­t kháº©u</h2>
        {error && <div className="p-2 bg-rose-50 text-rose-600 rounded">{error}</div>}
        <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-3">
          <input type="password" placeholder="Máº­t kháº©u hiá»‡n táº¡i" required value={form.oldPassword} onChange={e => setForm({...form, oldPassword: e.target.value})} className="w-full p-3 rounded border" />
          <input type="password" placeholder="Máº­t kháº©u má»›i" required value={form.newPassword} onChange={e => setForm({...form, newPassword: e.target.value})} className="w-full p-3 rounded border" />
          <input type="password" placeholder="Nháº­p láº¡i máº­t kháº©u má»›i" required value={form.confirm} onChange={e => setForm({...form, confirm: e.target.value})} className="w-full p-3 rounded border" />
          <button type="submit" className="w-full bg-emerald-600 text-white py-2 rounded">Äá»•i máº­t kháº©u</button>
        </form>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { useAuth } from '../../context/AuthContext.jsx';
import { usePersistentState } from '../../utils/persistence.js';
import { Lock, User, Terminal } from 'lucide-react';

export default function Login({ onFirstRun }) {
  const { login } = useAuth();
  const [form, setForm] = usePersistentState('login-form', { username: '', password: '' });
  const [error, setError] = useState('');
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);

  const handleSubmit = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setError('');
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      await login(form.username, form.password);
    } catch (err) {
      setError(err.response?.data?.error || 'KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ káº¿t ná»‘i Ä‘áº¿n mÃ¡y chá»§.');
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-slate-900 p-4">
      <div className="w-full max-w-sm bg-white p-6 rounded-2xl shadow-xl space-y-6">
        <div className="text-center space-y-1">
          <div className="inline-flex p-3 bg-emerald-50 text-emerald-600 rounded-xl mb-2">
            <Terminal size={24} />
          </div>
          <h1 className="text-base font-black text-slate-800 uppercase tracking-wider">Há»‡ thá»‘ng háº¡ch toÃ¡n ERP</h1>
          <p className="text-xs text-slate-400">ÄÄƒng nháº­p tÃ i khoáº£n káº¿ toÃ¡n doanh nghiá»‡p</p>
        </div>

        {error && (
          <div className="p-3 bg-rose-50 border border-rose-100 rounded-xl text-xs font-semibold text-rose-600">
            {error}
          </div>
        )}

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import api from '../../utils/api.js';
import { usePersistentState } from '../../utils/persistence.js';
import { ShieldCheck, Terminal } from 'lucide-react';

export default function Register({ onSwitch }) {
  const [form, setForm] = usePersistentState('register-form', { username: '', password: '' });
  const [success, setSuccess] = useState(false);

  const handleSubmit = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    try {
      const res = await api.post('/api/auth/register-admin', form);
      if (res.data.success) {
        setSuccess(true);
        setTimeout(() => onSwitch(), 2000);
      }
    } catch (err) {
      alert(err.response?.data?.error || 'Lá»—i Ä‘Äƒng kÃ½');
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-slate-900 p-4">

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { useVouchers } from '../../context/VoucherContext.jsx';
import { usePersistentState } from '../../utils/persistence.js';
import { Wallet, Plus, Trash2 } from 'lucide-react';

export default function CashManagement() {
  const { vouchers, createNewVoucher, removeVoucher } = useVouchers();
  const [form, setForm] = usePersistentState('cash-management-form', { date: '2026-01-01', desc: '', dr: '1111', cr: '131', amount: '' });

  const cashVouchers = vouchers.filter(v => v.voucher_type === 'Thu' || v.voucher_type === 'Chi');

  const handleSubmit = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    const type = (form.dr === '1111' || form.dr === '1121') ? 'Thu' : 'Chi';
    await createNewVoucher({
      voucherDate: form.date,
      description: form.desc,
      accountDr: form.dr,
      accountCr: form.cr,
      amount: parseFloat(form.amount),
      type
    });
    setForm({ date: '2026-01-01', desc: '', dr: '1111', cr: '131', amount: '' });
  };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      <h1 className="text-xl font-black text-slate-800 flex items-center gap-2"><Wallet className="text-emerald-600" size={24} /> PHÃ‚N Há»† QUá»¸ TIá»€N Máº¶T & TIá»€N Gá»¬I NGÃ‚N HÃ€NG</h1>

          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2">

            <input type="text" placeholder="TK CÃ³" value={form.cr} onChange={e => setForm({...form, cr: e.target.value})} className="w-full text-xs p-2.5 bg-slate-50 border rounded-xl font-mono" />

          <input type="number" placeholder="Sá»‘ tiá»n phÃ¡t sinh (VND)..." value={form.amount} onChange={e => setForm({...form, amount: e.target.value})} className="w-full text-xs p-2.5 bg-slate-50 border rounded-xl" />

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { useVouchers } from '../../context/VoucherContext.jsx';
import { BookOpenCheck, RefreshCw } from 'lucide-react';

export default function ClosingProcess() {
  const { vouchers, createNewVoucher } = useVouchers();
  const [log, setLog] = useState('');

  const executeClosing = async () => {
    setLog('Äang bÃ³c tÃ¡ch tá»•ng doanh thu (511) vÃ  giÃ¡ vá»‘n (632)...');
    
    let rev = 0, cogs = 0;
    vouchers.forEach(v => {
      if (v.account_cr === '5111') rev += parseFloat(v.amount);
      if (v.account_dr === '632') cogs += parseFloat(v.amount);
    });

    // PhÃ¡t sinh bÃºt toÃ¡n káº¿t chuyá»ƒn tá»± Ä‘á»™ng
    if (rev > 0) {
      await createNewVoucher({
        voucherDate: '2026-12-31',
        description: 'Káº¿t chuyá»ƒn doanh thu thuáº§n xÃ¡c Ä‘á»‹nh káº¿t quáº£ kinh doanh cuá»‘i ká»³',
        accountDr: '5111', accountCr: '911', amount: rev, type: 'Khac'
      });
    }
    if (cogs > 0) {
      await createNewVoucher({
        voucherDate: '2026-12-31',
        description: 'Káº¿t chuyá»ƒn chi phÃ­ giÃ¡ vá»‘n hÃ ng bÃ¡n cuá»‘i ká»³',
        accountDr: '911', accountCr: '632', amount: cogs, type: 'Khac'
      });
    }

    setLog(`KhÃ³a sá»• thÃ nh cÃ´ng! ÄÃ£ tá»± Ä‘á»™ng sinh bÃºt toÃ¡n káº¿t chuyá»ƒn doanh thu ${rev.toLocaleString()} Ä‘ vÃ  giÃ¡ vá»‘n ${cogs.toLocaleString()} Ä‘ sang tÃ i khoáº£n 911.`);
  };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      <h1 className="text-xl font-black text-slate-800 flex items-center gap-2"><BookOpenCheck className="text-indigo-600" size={24} /> KHÃ“A Sá»” Tá»° Äá»˜NG & Káº¾T CHUYá»‚N KINH DOANH CUá»I Ká»²</h1>
      <div className="bg-white p-6 rounded-2xl border shadow-sm max-w-xl space-y-4">
        <p className="text-xs text-slate-500 leading-relaxed">Há»‡ thá»‘ng quÃ©t toÃ n bá»™ Sá»• cÃ¡i, tá»± Ä‘á»™ng gom sá»‘ dÆ° tÃ i khoáº£n Doanh thu (511), Chi phÃ­ (632, 642) káº¿t chuyá»ƒn tá»± Ä‘á»™ng sang 911 Ä‘á»ƒ xÃ¡c Ä‘á»‹nh Tháº·ng dÆ°/ThÃ¢m há»¥t tÃ i chÃ­nh cá»§a doanh nghiá»‡p phÃ¡p nhÃ¢n.</p>

=== FILE: front-end\src\views\closing\OpeningBalances.jsx ===

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { useAuth } from '../../context/AuthContext.jsx';
import { CHART_OF_ACCOUNTS } from '../../utils/constants.js';
import api from '../../utils/api.js';
import { usePersistentState } from '../../utils/persistence.js';
import { Coins, Save } from 'lucide-react';

export default function OpeningBalances() {
  const { activeCompany } = useAuth();
  const [balances, setBalances] = usePersistentState('opening-balances-form', {});

  useEffect(() => {
    if (activeCompany) loadOpeningBalances();
  }, [activeCompany]);

  const loadOpeningBalances = async () => {
    try {
      const res = await api.get(`/api/opening-balances?company_id=${activeCompany}`);
      const initial = {};
      res.data.forEach(b => {
        initial[b.account_code] = { dr: b.debit_balance, cr: b.credit_balance };
      });
      setBalances(initial);
    } catch (err) { console.error(err); }
  };

  const handleInputChange = (code, field, val) => {
    setBalances({
      ...balances,
      [code]: { ...balances[code], [field]: val }
    });
  };

  const handleSave = async () => {
    try {
      const res = await api.post('/api/opening-balances', { companyId: activeCompany, balances });
      if (res.data.success) alert('LÆ°u sá»‘ dÆ° Ä‘áº§u ká»³ thÃ nh cÃ´ng!');
    } catch { alert('Lá»—i há»‡ thá»‘ng'); }
  };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between border-b pb-4">
        <h1 className="text-xl font-black text-slate-800 flex items-center gap-2"><Coins className="text-amber-500" size={24} /> KHAI BÃO Sá» DÆ¯ Äáº¦U Ká»² Há»† THá»NG TÃ€I KHOáº¢N TT200</h1>
        <button onClick={handleSave} className="bg-emerald-600 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-xl text-xs font-bold flex items-center gap-1.5 shadow-md"><Save size={16} /> LÆ°u báº£ng cÃ¢n Ä‘á»‘i sá»‘ dÆ°</button>
      </div>
      <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border shadow-sm overflow-hidden">
        <table className="w-full text-left text-xs">
          <thead>
            <tr className="bg-slate-50 font-bold border-b"><th className="p-3 w-32">MÃ£ tÃ i khoáº£n</th><th className="p-3">TÃªn tÃ i khoáº£n ThÃ´ng tÆ° 200</th><th className="p-3 text-center">DÆ° Ná»£ Ä‘áº§u ká»³</th><th className="p-3 text-center">DÆ° CÃ³ Ä‘áº§u ká»³</th></tr>
          </thead>
          <tbody className="divide-y">
            {CHART_OF_ACCOUNTS.map(acc => (
              <tr key={acc.code}>
                <td className="p-3 font-mono font-bold text-slate-600">{acc.code}</td>
                <td className="p-3 text-slate-700 font-medium">{acc.name}</td>
                <td className="p-3"><input type="number" placeholder="0" value={balances[acc.code]?.dr || ''} onChange={e => handleInputChange(acc.code, 'dr', e.target.value)} className="w-full p-2 bg-slate-50 border text-xs rounded-lg font-mono text-right" /></td>
                <td className="p-3"><input type="number" placeholder="0" value={balances[acc.code]?.cr || ''} onChange={e => handleInputChange(acc.code, 'cr', e.target.value)} className="w-full p-2 bg-slate-50 border text-xs rounded-lg font-mono text-right" /></td>
              </tr>
            ))}
          </tbody>
        </table>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

import { useVouchers } from '../../context/VoucherContext.jsx';
import { usePersistentState } from '../../utils/persistence.js';

export default function Payroll() {
  const { createNewVoucher } = useVouchers();
  const [salary, setSalary] = usePersistentState('payroll-form', '');

  const handleCalculatePayroll = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    if (!salary) return;
    const base = parseFloat(salary);
    const bhxh = Math.round(base * 0.105); // 10.5% trá»« lÆ°Æ¡ng ngÆ°á»i lao Ä‘á»™ng theo quy Ä‘á»‹nh phÃ¡p luáº­t

    // 1. TÃ­nh chi phÃ­ lÆ°Æ¡ng doanh nghiá»‡p gÃ¡nh chá»‹u
    await createNewVoucher({
      voucherDate: '2026-06-30',
      description: 'TrÃ­ch chi phÃ­ tiá»n lÆ°Æ¡ng pháº£i tráº£ bá»™ pháº­n quáº£n lÃ½ trong thÃ¡ng',
      accountDr: '6422', accountCr: '3341', amount: base, type: 'Khac'
    });

    // 2. Kháº¥u trá»« báº£o hiá»ƒm xÃ£ há»™i báº¯t buá»™c vÃ o lÆ°Æ¡ng ngÆ°á»i lao Ä‘á»™ng
    await createNewVoucher({
      voucherDate: '2026-06-30',
      description: 'TrÃ­ch kháº¥u trá»« báº£o hiá»ƒm báº¯t buá»™c (10.5%) vÃ o lÆ°Æ¡ng nhÃ¢n viÃªn',
      accountDr: '3341', accountCr: '3383', amount: bhxh, type: 'Khac'
    });

    alert('ÄÃ£ cháº¡y báº£ng lÆ°Æ¡ng tá»± Ä‘á»™ng vÃ  tá»± Ä‘á»™ng háº¡ch toÃ¡n ghi sá»• káº¿ toÃ¡n kÃ©p thÃ nh cÃ´ng!');
    setSalary('');
  };

      <div className="bg-white p-6 rounded-2xl border shadow-sm max-w-md space-y-4">

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { useVouchers } from '../../context/VoucherContext.jsx';
import { usePersistentState } from '../../utils/persistence.js';
import { ShoppingBag, Plus } from 'lucide-react';

export default function PurchaseInventory() {
  const { createNewVoucher } = useVouchers();
  const [form, setForm] = usePersistentState('purchase-inventory-form', { item: '', amount: '', tax: '10' });

  const handlePurchase = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    const baseAmount = parseFloat(form.amount);
    const taxAmount = Math.round(baseAmount * (parseFloat(form.tax) / 100));
    const totalPay = baseAmount + taxAmount;

    // Háº¡ch toÃ¡n tiá»n mua hÃ ng hÃ³a nguyÃªn váº­t liá»‡u nháº­p kho
    await createNewVoucher({
      voucherDate: '2026-01-15',
      description: `Nháº­p kho váº­t tÆ° hÃ ng hÃ³a: ${form.item}`,
      accountDr: '156', accountCr: '331', amount: baseAmount, type: 'Nhap'
    });

    // Háº¡ch toÃ¡n thuáº¿ GTGT Ä‘áº§u vÃ o Ä‘Æ°á»£c kháº¥u trá»«
    if (taxAmount > 0) {
      await createNewVoucher({
        voucherDate: '2026-01-15',
        description: `Thuáº¿ GTGT Ä‘áº§u vÃ o Ä‘Æ°á»£c kháº¥u trá»« cá»§a hÃ³a Ä‘Æ¡n mua hÃ ng ${form.item}`,
        accountDr: '1331', accountCr: '331', amount: taxAmount, type: 'Khac'
      });
    }

    alert(`ÄÃ£ háº¡ch toÃ¡n nháº­p kho hÃ ng hÃ³a. Tá»•ng sá»‘ tiá»n pháº£i tráº£ nhÃ  cung cáº¥p (331): ${totalPay.toLocaleString()} Ä‘`);
    setForm({ item: '', amount: '', tax: '10' });
  };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      <h1 className="text-xl font-black text-slate-800 flex items-center gap-2"><ShoppingBag className="text-emerald-600" size={24} /> PHÃ‚N Há»† MUA HÃ€NG VÃ€ Háº CH TOÃN Váº¬T TÆ¯ NHáº¬P KHO</h1>
      <form onSubmit={handlePurchase} className="bg-white p-5 rounded-2xl border shadow-sm max-w-md space-y-3">
        <input type="text" placeholder="TÃªn nguyÃªn váº­t liá»‡u / HÃ ng hÃ³a nháº­p kho..." value={form.item} onChange={e => setForm({...form, item: e.target.value})} className="w-full text-xs p-2.5 bg-slate-50 border rounded-xl" />
        <input type="number" placeholder="GiÃ¡ trá»‹ mua trÆ°á»›c thuáº¿ (VND)..." value={form.amount} onChange={e => setForm({...form, amount: e.target.value})} className="w-full text-xs p-2.5 bg-slate-50 border rounded-xl" />
        <select value={form.tax} onChange={e => setForm({...form, tax: e.target.value})} className="w-full text-xs p-2.5 bg-slate-50 border rounded-xl">
          <option value="0">Thuáº¿ suáº¥t GTGT: 0%</option>
          <option value="5">Thuáº¿ suáº¥t GTGT: 5%</option>
          <option value="10">Thuáº¿ suáº¥t GTGT: 10%</option>
        </select>
        <button type="submit" className="w-full bg-emerald-600 text-white font-bold text-xs py-2.5 rounded-xl"><Plus size={14} className="inline mr-1" /> PhÃ¡t hÃ nh chá»©ng tá»« mua kho</button>
      </form>
    </div>
  );
}

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { useVouchers } from '../../context/VoucherContext.jsx';
import { Layers, FileSpreadsheet } from 'lucide-react';

export default function AutoSalesExcel() {
  const { createNewVoucher } = useVouchers();
  const [simulatedRows, setSimulatedRows] = useState([]);

  const handleSyncAll = async () => {
    for (const row of simulatedRows) {
      await createNewVoucher({
        voucherDate: '2026-04-01',
        description: `Doanh thu bÃ¡n hÃ ng hÃ³a tá»± Ä‘á»™ng tá»« Excel cho ${row.customer}`,
        accountDr: '131', accountCr: '5111', amount: row.amount, type: 'Xuan'
      });
    }
    alert('ÄÃ£ xá»­ lÃ½ Ä‘á»“ng bá»™ chuá»—i hÃ³a Ä‘Æ¡n Excel vÃ  tá»± Ä‘á»™ng sinh sá»• cÃ¡i háº¡ch toÃ¡n Ná»£ 131 / CÃ³ 5111 thÃ nh cÃ´ng!');
    setSimulatedRows([]);
  };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      <h1 className="text-xl font-black text-slate-800 flex items-center gap-2"><Layers className="text-emerald-600" size={24} /> Äá»’NG Bá»˜ DOANH THU HOÃ ÄÆ N HÃ€NG LOáº T Tá»ª EXCEL</h1>
      <div className="bg-white p-5 rounded-2xl border shadow-sm space-y-4">
        <div className="p-4 border-2 border-dashed border-slate-200 rounded-xl flex flex-col items-center justify-center text-center p-6 bg-slate-50">
          <FileSpreadsheet className="text-emerald-600 mb-2" size={32} />
          <span className="text-xs font-semibold text-slate-600">Há»‡ thá»‘ng sáºµn sÃ ng phÃ¢n tÃ¡ch luá»“ng dá»¯ liá»‡u Excel bÃ¡n ra</span>
        </div>
        {simulatedRows.length > 0 && (
          <div className="space-y-2">
            <button onClick={handleSyncAll} className="bg-emerald-600 text-white font-bold text-xs px-4 py-2 rounded-xl">Äá»“ng bá»™ ghi sá»• toÃ n bá»™ dá»¯ liá»‡u Excel ({simulatedRows.length} hÃ ng)</button>
            <div className="border rounded-xl overflow-hidden text-xs">
              {simulatedRows.map(r => (
                <div key={r.id} className="p-2 border-b flex justify-between bg-white">
                  <span>{r.id} - <b>{r.customer}</b></span>
                  <span className="font-mono font-bold text-slate-700">{r.amount.toLocaleString()} Ä‘</span>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}


=== FILE: front-end\src\views\sales\ItemManagement.jsx ===

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { Package, Plus, Trash2, RefreshCw } from 'lucide-react';
import { useAuth } from '../../context/AuthContext.jsx';
import api from '../../utils/api.js';
import { usePersistentState } from '../../utils/persistence.js';

export default function ItemManagement() {
  const { activeCompany } = useAuth(); // Theo dÃµi cÃ´ng ty Ä‘ang lÃ m viá»‡c tá»« Header
  const [items, setItems] = useState([]);
  const [form, setForm] = usePersistentState('item-management-form', { code: '', name: '', unit: 'CÃ¡i' });
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState('');
  const [success, setSuccess] = useState('');

  // Tá»± Ä‘á»™ng táº£i láº¡i danh sÃ¡ch khi vÃ o phÃ¢n há»‡ hoáº·c khi ngÆ°á»i dÃ¹ng chuyá»ƒn Ä‘á»•i cÃ´ng ty
  useEffect(() => {
    if (activeCompany) {
      fetchItems();
    }
  }, [activeCompany]);

  // 1. Äá»ŒC DANH SÃCH: ÄÃ£ bá»• sung tham sá»‘ ?company_id phá»¥c vá»¥ tÃ i khoáº£n Admin xem chÃ©o
  const fetchItems = async () => {
    if (!activeCompany) return;
    setLoading(true);
    setError('');
    try {
      const res = await api.get(`/api/items?company_id=${activeCompany}`);
      setItems(res.data);
    } catch (err) {
      setError(err.response?.data?.error || 'KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ káº¿t ná»‘i láº¥y danh má»¥c váº­t tÆ°!');
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };

  // 2. THÃŠM Má»šI Váº¬T TÆ¯: Gá»­i kÃ¨m companyId Ä‘á»ƒ Backend nháº­n diá»‡n Ä‘Ãºng thá»±c thá»ƒ háº¡ch toÃ¡n
  const handleAdd = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    if (!activeCompany) {
      setError('Vui lÃ²ng chá»n má»™t doanh nghiá»‡p trÃªn thanh cÃ´ng cá»¥ trÆ°á»›c!');
      return;
    }
    setError('');
    setSuccess('');
    
    try {
      const res = await api.post('/api/items', {
        code: form.code.toUpperCase().trim(), // Chuáº©n hÃ³a viáº¿t hoa mÃ£ SKU
        name: form.name.trim(),
        unit: form.unit.trim(),
        companyId: activeCompany // Truyá»n mÃ£ doanh nghiá»‡p hiá»‡n táº¡i
      });
      
      if (res.data.success) {
        setSuccess('ÄÄƒng kÃ½ mÃ£ váº­t tÆ° má»›i thÃ nh cÃ´ng!');
        setForm({ code: '', name: '', unit: 'CÃ¡i' });
        fetchItems(); // Táº£i láº¡i danh sÃ¡ch sau khi lÆ°u
      }
    } catch (err) {
      setError(err.response?.data?.error || 'Lá»—i há»‡ thá»‘ng khi Ä‘Äƒng kÃ½ váº­t tÆ°!');
    }
  };

  // 3. XÃ“A Váº¬T TÆ¯: Truyá»n company_id qua URL Ä‘á»ƒ khá»›p chÃ­nh xÃ¡c vá»›i KhÃ³a chÃ­nh phá»©c há»£p á»Ÿ DB
  const handleDelete = async (code) => {
    if (!window.confirm(`XÃ³a sáº£n pháº©m "${code}"? HÃ nh Ä‘á»™ng nÃ y khÃ´ng thá»ƒ hoÃ n tÃ¡c.`)) return;
    setError('');
    setSuccess('');

    try {
      const res = await api.delete(`/api/items/${code}?company_id=${activeCompany}`);
      if (res.data.success) {
        setSuccess('ÄÃ£ xÃ³a váº­t tÆ° thÃ nh cÃ´ng khá»i há»‡ thá»‘ng!');
        fetchItems(); // Táº£i láº¡i danh sÃ¡ch sau khi xÃ³a
      }
    } catch (err) {
      setError(err.response?.data?.error || 'KhÃ´ng cÃ³ quyá»n hoáº·c lá»—i khi xÃ³a váº­t tÆ° nÃ y!');
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
        <h1 className="text-xl font-black text-slate-800 flex items-center gap-2">
          <Package className="text-amber-600" size={24} /> 
          DANH Má»¤C MÃƒ Váº¬T TÆ¯, Sáº¢N PHáº¨M HÃ€NG HÃ“A Tá»’N KHO
        </h1>
        <button 
          onClick={fetchItems} 
          disabled={loading}
          className="p-2 hover:bg-slate-100 rounded-xl text-slate-500 transition-all flex items-center gap-1 text-xs font-semibold border bg-white"
          title="Táº£i láº¡i danh sÃ¡ch"
        >
          <RefreshCw size={14} className={loading ? 'animate-spin text-amber-600' : ''} />
          {loading ? 'Äang táº£i...' : 'LÃ m má»›i'}
        </button>
      </div>

      {/* Box Hiá»ƒn thá»‹ thÃ´ng bÃ¡o tráº¡ng thÃ¡i */}
      {error && (
        <div className="p-3 bg-rose-50 border border-rose-200 text-rose-600 text-xs font-bold rounded-xl animate-fade-in">
          âš ï¸ {error}
        </div>
      )}
      {success && (
        <div className="p-3 bg-emerald-50 border border-emerald-200 text-emerald-600 text-xs font-bold rounded-xl animate-fade-in">
          âœ… {success}
        </div>
      )}

      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-3 gap-6">
        {/* Form ÄÄƒng kÃ½ */}
        <form onSubmit={handleAdd} className="bg-white p-5 rounded-2xl border shadow-sm space-y-3 h-fit">
          <h3 className="text-xs font-black text-slate-700 uppercase tracking-wider mb-1">Khai bÃ¡o mÃ£ má»›i</h3>
          <div>
            <label className="block text-[10px] font-bold text-slate-400 mb-1 uppercase tracking-wider">MÃ£ Váº­t TÆ° (SKU)</label>
            <input 
              type="text" 
              placeholder="VÃ­ dá»¥: NVL001, SP002..." 
              required 
              value={form.code} 
              onChange={e => setForm({...form, code: e.target.value})} 
              className="w-full text-xs p-2.5 bg-slate-50 border rounded-xl font-semibold focus:outline-none focus:border-amber-500 transition" 
            />
          </div>
          <div>
            <label className="block text-[10px] font-bold text-slate-400 mb-1 uppercase tracking-wider">TÃªn quy cÃ¡ch</label>
            <input 
              type="text" 
              placeholder="TÃªn chi tiáº¿t sáº£n pháº©m..." 
              required 
              value={form.name} 
              onChange={e => setForm({...form, name: e.target.value})} 
              className="w-full text-xs p-2.5 bg-slate-50 border rounded-xl font-semibold focus:outline-none focus:border-amber-500 transition" 
            />
          </div>
          <div>
            <label className="block text-[10px] font-bold text-slate-400 mb-1 uppercase tracking-wider">ÄÆ¡n vá»‹ tÃ­nh</label>
            <input 
              type="text" 
              placeholder="CÃ¡i, Kg, ThÃ¹ng, MÃ©t..." 
              required 
              value={form.unit} 
              onChange={e => setForm({...form, unit: e.target.value})} 
              className="w-full text-xs p-2.5 bg-slate-50 border rounded-xl font-semibold focus:outline-none focus:border-amber-500 transition" 
            />
          </div>
          <button 
            type="submit" 
            disabled={loading}
            className="w-full bg-amber-600 hover:bg-amber-700 transition text-white font-bold text-xs py-2.5 rounded-xl shadow-sm flex items-center justify-center gap-1"
          >
            <Plus size={16} /> ÄÄƒng kÃ½ mÃ£ má»›i
          </button>
        </form>

        {/* Báº£ng Dá»¯ Liá»‡u Thá»±c */}
        <div className="bg-white p-5 rounded-2xl border shadow-sm col-span-2 overflow-hidden">
          <div className="overflow-x-auto">
            <table className="w-full text-left text-xs border-collapse">
              <thead>
                <tr className="bg-slate-50 font-bold border-b text-slate-500">

=== FILE: front-end\src\views\tax\TaxReporting.jsx ===

import React from 'react';
import { useVouchers } from '../../context/VoucherContext.jsx';
import { Percent, Landmark } from 'lucide-react';

export default function TaxReporting() {
  const { vouchers } = useVouchers();

  let vatInput = 0;  // Thuáº¿ GTGT Ä‘áº§u vÃ o Ä‘Æ°á»£c kháº¥u trá»« (1331)
  let vatOutput = 0; // Thuáº¿ GTGT Ä‘áº§u ra pháº£i ná»™p (3331)

  vouchers.forEach(v => {
    if (v.account_dr === '1331') vatInput += parseFloat(v.amount);
    if (v.account_cr === '3331') vatOutput += parseFloat(v.amount);
  });

  const payableVat = vatOutput - vatInput;

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      <h1 className="text-xl font-black text-slate-800 flex items-center gap-2"><Percent className="text-rose-600" size={24} /> Tá»œ KHAI Tá»”NG Há»¢P NGHÄ¨A Vá»¤ THUáº¾ GTGT (MáºªU 01/GTGT)</h1>
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-3 gap-6">
        <div className="bg-white p-5 rounded-2xl border shadow-sm">
          <span className="text-[10px] font-bold text-slate-400 uppercase block">Thuáº¿ GTGT Ä‘áº§u vÃ o tÃ­ch lÅ©y (TK 1331)</span>
          <h3 className="text-lg font-black text-emerald-600">{vatInput.toLocaleString()} Ä‘</h3>
        </div>
        <div className="bg-white p-5 rounded-2xl border shadow-sm">
          <span className="text-[10px] font-bold text-slate-400 uppercase block">Thuáº¿ GTGT Ä‘áº§u ra phÃ¡t sinh (TK 3331)</span>
          <h3 className="text-lg font-black text-orange-600">{vatOutput.toLocaleString()} Ä‘</h3>
        </div>
        <div className="bg-white p-5 rounded-2xl border shadow-sm bg-slate-900 text-white">
          <span className="text-[10px] font-bold text-slate-400 uppercase block text-slate-400">NghÄ©a vá»¥ Thuáº¿ GTGT cuá»‘i ká»³ pháº£i ná»™p ngÃ¢n sÃ¡ch</span>
          <h3 className="text-lg font-black text-white">{payableVat > 0 ? `${payableVat.toLocaleString()} Ä‘` : '0 Ä‘ (CÃ²n Ä‘Æ°á»£c kháº¥u trá»« chuyá»ƒn ká»³ sau)'}</h3>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

=== FILE: PROJECT_FOR_GEMINI.txt ===

KETOAN ERP - PROJECT SUMMARY (Prepared for Gemini Pro upload)

Repository: ketoan-erp
Location: root of workspace
Date: 2026-07-01

OVERVIEW
--------
Ketoan ERP is a multi-company accounting system (Vietnamese, TT200). It contains a Node.js/Express backend using PostgreSQL and a React + Vite frontend with Tailwind CSS.

GOAL OF THIS FILE
-----------------
Provide a comprehensive, self-contained text summary of the project (structure, run instructions, env vars, key endpoints, recent changes) so it can be uploaded to Gemini Pro for inspection.

TECH STACK
----------
- Backend: Node.js (ES Modules), Express, JWT, bcryptjs, pg (Postgres)
- Frontend: React 18, Vite, Tailwind CSS
- DB: PostgreSQL
- Dev: npm, node

PROJECT STRUCTURE (top-level)
-----------------------------
- backend/
  - server.js                # Main Express app, DB migration/auto-ALTER, API endpoints
  - schema.sql               # SQL schema (present)
  - package.json
  - .env.example
- front-end/
  - src/
    - App.jsx
    - main.jsx
    - index.css
    - components/            # Header, Sidebar, MainContent, ResponsiveContainer
    - context/
      - AuthContext.jsx      # Central auth and loadUsers() used by UI
      - VoucherContext.jsx
    - views/                 # All UI views by module (admin, auth, cash, closing...)
      - admin/
        - CompanyManagement.jsx  # Admin UI for users & companies (modified)
      - auth/
        - Login.jsx
        - Register.jsx
        - ChangePassword.jsx
  - vite.config.js
  - package.json

KEY FILES & PURPOSE
-------------------
- backend/server.js
  - Initializes DB tables (companies, users, user_companies, sessions, etc.)
  - Provides auth endpoints: /api/auth/register-admin, /api/auth/login, /api/auth/logout
  - User management: /api/users, POST /api/users, DELETE /api/users/:id
  - Company management: /api/companies
  - Uses JWT + sessions table to validate tokens via `authenticate` middleware

- front-end/src/context/AuthContext.jsx
  - Holds `token`, `user`, `companies`, `users` state
  - Exposes `loadUsers()` used by components instead of calling API directly
  - Manages `activeCompany` in localStorage and `token` in sessionStorage

- front-end/src/views/admin/CompanyManagement.jsx
  - Admin UI for creating users, assigning companies, resetting passwords
  - Now uses `loadUsers()` from `AuthContext` to derive `localUsers`

- front-end/src/components/MainContent.jsx
  - Central place that loads data for tabs including the users management tab
  - Updated to use `loadUsers()` instead of direct API calls

RECENT CHANGES
--------------
- Replaced direct `/api/users` calls in multiple components with `AuthContext.loadUsers()` to keep a single source of truth for users and avoid race conditions where hiding admin could appear to clear user lists.
- Files modified and pushed to `main` branch:
  - front-end/src/views/admin/CompanyManagement.jsx
  - front-end/src/components/MainContent.jsx
- Commit message: "fix(users): use AuthContext.loadUsers to keep user list stable when admin hidden"

ENVIRONMENT & REQUIRED VARIABLES
--------------------------------
- backend/.env (copy from .env.example)
  - DATABASE_URL=postgresql://<user>:<pass>@<host>:<port>/<db>
  - JWT_SECRET=<a very long secret string>
  - PORT (optional, default 5000)
- front-end/.env (optional)
  - VITE_API_URL=http://localhost:5000

LOCAL SETUP & RUN (QUICK)
-------------------------
1) Backend
   - cd backend
   - npm install
   - Create `.env` from `.env.example`, set `DATABASE_URL` and `JWT_SECRET`.
   - Start server (dev): `node server.js` or `npm run dev` (requires nodemon globally)
   - Health check: GET http://localhost:5000/api/health

2) Frontend
   - cd front-end
   - npm install
   - Create `.env` (optional) with `VITE_API_URL=http://localhost:5000`
   - Start dev server: `npm run dev` (Vite default port 3000)
   - Open http://localhost:3000

TESTING THE USER LIST (ADMIN FLOW)
----------------------------------
1. Create admin (only first-run): POST /api/auth/register-admin {username, password}
2. Login: POST /api/auth/login -> receive token and user payload (saved to sessionStorage by UI)
3. The UI (AuthContext) calls `loadUsers()` during login; components read from context and render lists.
4. Verify Admin views:
   - Open Admin â†’ "Cáº¥u hÃ¬nh há»‡ thá»‘ng phÃ¡p nhÃ¢n" or tab 'Quáº£n lÃ½ Ã´ tÃ­ch phÃ¢n quyá»n'
   - Confirm user list shows admin, KTT, NV as applicable

NOTES & TROUBLESHOOTING
-----------------------
- If users are not visible: verify backend `/api/users` returns rows when called with Authorization header (Bearer token). If direct API returns empty, then investigate DB records or the SQL query filtering by role or manager.
- Session handling: tokens are validated against `sessions` table; ensure the session row exists after login.
- If using `npm run dev` for backend, `nodemon` must be installed globally or as a dev dependency.

PACKING THE PROJECT FOR UPLOAD
------------------------------
If Gemini Pro requires a single file, you can create a compressed archive (zip) of the repository. Example (Windows PowerShell):

```powershell
cd "c:\Users\proge\OneDrive\MÃ¡y tÃ­nh\tools\Ketoan"
Compress-Archive -Path . -DestinationPath ..\ketoan-erp.zip
```

Or produce a plain text representation (file listings + important files appended) â€” this text summary is intended for that.

ADDITIONAL ACTIONS I CAN TAKE
-----------------------------
- Create a full project dump text file (concatenate every source file into one large `.txt`) and place it in the repo root (useful if Gemini Pro accepts only text). WARNING: this may be very large.
- Create a zip archive of the repo and push it to a remote location.
- Start backend + frontend here and run an end-to-end test (I can attempt to run them if you want â€” note: environment must be configured locally).

CONTACT/USAGE NOTES
-------------------
- File created by automation to facilitate upload to Gemini Pro. If you want the entire source concatenated into a single big `.txt` file, say "concat all files into one text file" and I will produce it (may take time and produce a large file).

## **ðŸ› Troubleshooting**

### **Backend error: Cannot find module 'dotenv'**
```bash
cd backend && npm install dotenv
```

### **Frontend error: VITE_API_URL undefined**
```bash
# Táº¡o file .env
echo "VITE_API_URL=http://localhost:5000" > front-end/.env
```

### **PostgreSQL connection refused**
```bash
# Kiá»ƒm tra PostgreSQL Ä‘ang cháº¡y
# macOS: brew services list
# Windows: Kiá»ƒm tra Services -> PostgreSQL
# Linux: sudo systemctl status postgresql
```

### **Port 5000 already in use**
```bash
# Kill process trÃªn port 5000
# Windows: netstat -ano | findstr :5000
# Linux: lsof -i :5000 | grep LISTEN | awk '{print $2}' | xargs kill
```

<file path="backend/schema.sql">
-- ====================================================================
-- Cáº¤U TRÃšC CÆ  Sá»ž Dá»® LIá»†U Há»† THá»NG KETOAN ERP - THÃ”NG TÆ¯ 200/2014/TT-BTC
-- ====================================================================

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS companies (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    tax_code VARCHAR(50) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    address TEXT,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    username VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    password TEXT NOT NULL,
    role VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'nv', -- admin (Quáº£n trá»‹), ktt (Káº¿ toÃ¡n trÆ°á»Ÿng), nv (NhÃ¢n viÃªn)
    company_id INT REFERENCES companies(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS accounts (
    code VARCHAR(20) PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL -- Tai San, Nguon Von, Doanh Thu, Chi Phi, Trung Gian
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS opening_balances (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    company_id INT REFERENCES companies(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    account_code VARCHAR(20) REFERENCES accounts(code) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    debit_balance NUMERIC(15,2) DEFAULT 0,
    credit_balance NUMERIC(15,2) DEFAULT 0,
    fiscal_year INT NOT NULL,
    UNIQUE(company_id, account_code, fiscal_year)
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS vouchers (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    company_id INT REFERENCES companies(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    voucher_date DATE NOT NULL,
    description TEXT NOT NULL,
    account_dr VARCHAR(20) REFERENCES accounts(code),
    account_cr VARCHAR(20) REFERENCES accounts(code),
    amount NUMERIC(15,2) NOT NULL,
    voucher_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL, -- Thu, Chi, Nhap, Xuan, Khac
    created_by INT REFERENCES users(id),
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- ====================================================================
-- Náº P DANH Má»¤C TÃ€I KHOáº¢N CHI TIáº¾T THEO THÃ”NG TÆ¯ 200
-- ====================================================================

<file path="front-end/src/context/VoucherContext.jsx">
import React, { createContext, useContext, useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { useAuth } from './AuthContext.jsx';
import api from '../utils/api.js';

// 1. Khá»Ÿi táº¡o Context ná»™i bá»™ (KhÃ´ng export trá»±c tiáº¿p dÃ²ng nÃ y)
const VoucherContext = createContext(null);

// 2. Äá»‹nh nghÄ©a Component Provider (Viáº¿t hoa chá»¯ cÃ¡i Ä‘áº§u)
export function VoucherProvider({ children }) {
  const { activeCompany } = useAuth();
  const [vouchers, setVouchers] = useState([]);
  const [isSyncing, setIsSyncing] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (activeCompany) {
      loadVouchers();
    } else {
      setVouchers([]);
    }
  }, [activeCompany]);

  const loadVouchers = async () => {
    setIsSyncing(true);
    try {
      const res = await api.get(`/api/vouchers?company_id=${activeCompany}`);
      setVouchers(res.data);
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Lá»—i táº£i danh sÃ¡ch chá»©ng tá»«:', err);
    } finally {
      setIsSyncing(false);
    }
  };

  const createNewVoucher = async (data) => {
    try {
      const res = await api.post('/api/vouchers', { ...data, companyId: activeCompany });
      if (res.data.success) {
        setVouchers(prev => [res.data.voucher, ...prev]);
        return { success: true };
      }
    } catch (err) {
      return { success: false, error: err.response?.data?.error || err.message };
    }
  };

  const removeVoucher = async (id) => {
    try {
      const res = await api.delete(`/api/vouchers/${id}`);
      if (res.data.success) {
        setVouchers(prev => prev.filter(v => v.id !== id));
        return { success: true, message: res.data.message };
      }
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Lá»—i xÃ³a chá»©ng tá»«:', err);
      // Tráº£ vá» thÃ´ng bÃ¡o lá»—i chi tiáº¿t tá»« Backend (VÃ­ dá»¥: "Báº¡n khÃ´ng cÃ³ quyá»n thá»±c hiá»‡n...")
      return { 
        success: false, 
        error: err.response?.data?.error || err.message || 'Lá»—i khÃ´ng thá»ƒ xÃ³a chá»©ng tá»«' 
      };
    }
  };

  return (
    <VoucherContext.Provider value={{ vouchers, isSyncing, createNewVoucher, removeVoucher, reloadVouchers: loadVouchers }}>
      {children}
    </VoucherContext.Provider>
  );
}

// 3. Khá»Ÿi táº¡o Custom Hook ná»™i bá»™
function useVouchers() {
  const context = useContext(VoucherContext);
  if (!context) {
    throw new Error('useVouchers pháº£i Ä‘Æ°á»£c lá»“ng bÃªn trong cáº¥u trÃºc cá»§a VoucherProvider');
  }
  return context;
}

// ==========================================
// Báº®T BUá»˜C CHO VITE: Export táº­p trung táº¥t cáº£ hook thuáº§n á»Ÿ cuá»‘i file
// ==========================================
export { useVouchers };
// ==========================================
</file>

import React from 'react';
import ReactDOM from 'react-dom/client';
import App from './App.jsx';
import './index.css';
import { AuthProvider } from './context/AuthContext.jsx';
import { VoucherProvider } from './context/VoucherContext.jsx';

ReactDOM.createRoot(document.getElementById('root')).render(
  <React.StrictMode>
    <AuthProvider>
      <VoucherProvider>
        <App />
      </VoucherProvider>
    </AuthProvider>
  </React.StrictMode>

<file path="front-end/src/utils/accountingEngine.js">
/**
 * Bá»™ engine tÃ­nh toÃ¡n sá»‘ dÆ° Ä‘á»™ng tá»« chá»©ng tá»« (T-Account Ledger Flow)
 */
export function calculateBalances(vouchers, openingBalances = []) {
  const ledger = {};

  // Khá»Ÿi táº¡o sá»‘ dÆ° Ä‘áº§u ká»³ tá»« thiáº¿t láº­p cáº¥u hÃ¬nh
  openingBalances.forEach(bal => {
    ledger[bal.account_code] = {
      dr: parseFloat(bal.debit_balance || 0),
      cr: parseFloat(bal.credit_balance || 0)
    };
  });

  // Cá»™ng dá»“n lÅ©y káº¿ phÃ¡t sinh bÃªn Ná»£ vÃ  phÃ¡t sinh bÃªn CÃ³ tá»« tá»‡p chá»©ng tá»« gá»‘c
  vouchers.forEach(v => {
    const amount = parseFloat(v.amount || 0);
    
    if (!ledger[v.account_dr]) ledger[v.account_dr] = { dr: 0, cr: 0 };
    if (!ledger[v.account_cr]) ledger[v.account_cr] = { dr: 0, cr: 0 };

    ledger[v.account_dr].dr += amount;
    ledger[v.account_cr].cr += amount;
  });

  return ledger;
}
</file>

import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import api from '../../utils/api.js';
import { Trash2, Building2 } from 'lucide-react';

export default function CompanyList({ companies, onRefresh }) {
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);

  const handleDeleteCompany = async (companyId, companyName) => {
    if (!window.confirm(`Báº¡n cÃ³ cháº¯c cháº¯n muá»‘n xÃ³a cÃ´ng ty "${companyName}"? HÃ nh Ä‘á»™ng nÃ y khÃ´ng thá»ƒ hoÃ n tÃ¡c!`)) {
      return;
    }

    setLoading(true);
    try {
      await api.delete(`/api/companies/${companyId}`);
      alert('ÄÃ£ xÃ³a cÃ´ng ty thÃ nh cÃ´ng!');
      onRefresh();
    } catch (err) {
      alert(err.response?.data?.error || 'Lá»—i xÃ³a cÃ´ng ty!');
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };

  if (!companies || companies.length === 0) {
    return (
      <div className="bg-white p-5 rounded-2xl border border-slate-200 shadow-sm">
        <h3 className="text-xs font-bold text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider flex items-center gap-1.5 mb-4">
          <Building2 size={16} className="text-blue-600" /> Danh sÃ¡ch cÃ´ng ty / PhÃ¡p nhÃ¢n
        </h3>
        <p className="text-sm text-slate-500 text-center py-6">ChÆ°a cÃ³ cÃ´ng ty nÃ o. Vui lÃ²ng thÃªm cÃ´ng ty má»›i bÃªn trÃªn.</p>
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className="bg-white p-5 rounded-2xl border border-slate-200 shadow-sm space-y-4">
      <h3 className="text-xs font-bold text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider flex items-center gap-1.5">
        <Building2 size={16} className="text-blue-600" /> Danh sÃ¡ch cÃ´ng ty / PhÃ¡p nhÃ¢n
      </h3>
      <div className="overflow-x-auto">
        <table className="w-full text-left border-collapse text-xs">
          <thead>
            <tr className="bg-slate-50 border-b border-slate-200 font-bold text-slate-600">
              <th className="p-3">TÃªn cÃ´ng ty</th>
              <th className="p-3">MÃ£ sá»‘ thuáº¿</th>
              <th className="p-3">Äá»‹a chá»‰</th>
              <th className="p-3 text-center">HÃ nh Ä‘á»™ng</th>
            </tr>
          </thead>
          <tbody className="divide-y divide-slate-100">
            {companies.map(company => (
              <tr key={company.id} className="hover:bg-slate-50/50 transition">
                <td className="p-3 font-bold text-slate-700">{company.name}</td>
                <td className="p-3 text-slate-600">{company.tax_code}</td>
                <td className="p-3 text-slate-600">{company.address || '--'}</td>

                    disabled={loading}

                    <Trash2 size={15} />

          </tbody>

<file path="front-end/src/views/auth/ChangePassword.jsx">
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { useAuth } from '../../context/AuthContext.jsx';

export default function ChangePassword() {
  const { changePassword } = useAuth();
  const [form, setForm] = useState({ oldPassword: '', newPassword: '', confirm: '' });
  const [error, setError] = useState('');
  const [success, setSuccess] = useState(false);

  const handleSubmit = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setError('');
    if (form.newPassword !== form.confirm) return setError('Máº­t kháº©u má»›i khÃ´ng khá»›p');
    try {
      await changePassword(form.oldPassword, form.newPassword);
      setSuccess(true);
    } catch (err) { setError(err); }
  };

  if (success) return (
    <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-slate-50 p-4">
      <div className="w-full max-w-md bg-white p-6 rounded-2xl shadow text-center">
        <h2 className="text-lg font-black text-emerald-600">Äá»•i máº­t kháº©u thÃ nh cÃ´ng</h2>
        <p className="text-sm text-slate-600 mt-2">Vui lÃ²ng Ä‘Äƒng nháº­p láº¡i náº¿u cáº§n.</p>
        <button onClick={() => location.reload()} className="mt-4 bg-emerald-600 text-white py-2 px-4 rounded">Äá»“ng Ã½</button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-slate-50 p-4">
      <div className="w-full max-w-md bg-white p-6 rounded-2xl shadow space-y-4">
        <h2 className="text-base font-black text-slate-800">Thay Ä‘á»•i máº­t kháº©u</h2>
        {error && <div className="p-2 bg-rose-50 text-rose-600 rounded">{error}</div>}
        <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-3">
          <input type="password" placeholder="Máº­t kháº©u hiá»‡n táº¡i" required value={form.oldPassword} onChange={e => setForm({...form, oldPassword: e.target.value})} className="w-full p-3 rounded border" />
          <input type="password" placeholder="Máº­t kháº©u má»›i" required value={form.newPassword} onChange={e => setForm({...form, newPassword: e.target.value})} className="w-full p-3 rounded border" />
          <input type="password" placeholder="Nháº­p láº¡i máº­t kháº©u má»›i" required value={form.confirm} onChange={e => setForm({...form, confirm: e.target.value})} className="w-full p-3 rounded border" />
          <button type="submit" className="w-full bg-emerald-600 text-white py-2 rounded">Äá»•i máº­t kháº©u</button>
        </form>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

<file path="front-end/src/views/cash/CashManagement.jsx">
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { useVouchers } from '../../context/VoucherContext.jsx';
import { Wallet, Plus, Trash2 } from 'lucide-react';

export default function CashManagement() {
  const { vouchers, createNewVoucher, removeVoucher } = useVouchers();
  const [form, setForm] = useState({ date: '2026-01-01', desc: '', dr: '1111', cr: '131', amount: '' });

  const cashVouchers = vouchers.filter(v => v.voucher_type === 'Thu' || v.voucher_type === 'Chi');

  const handleSubmit = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    const type = (form.dr === '1111' || form.dr === '1121') ? 'Thu' : 'Chi';
    await createNewVoucher({
      voucherDate: form.date,
      description: form.desc,
      accountDr: form.dr,
      accountCr: form.cr,
      amount: parseFloat(form.amount),
      type
    });
    setForm({ date: '2026-01-01', desc: '', dr: '1111', cr: '131', amount: '' });
  };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      <h1 className="text-xl font-black text-slate-800 flex items-center gap-2"><Wallet className="text-emerald-600" size={24} /> PHÃ‚N Há»† QUá»¸ TIá»€N Máº¶T & TIá»€N Gá»¬I NGÃ‚N HÃ€NG</h1>
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-6">
        <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="bg-white p-5 rounded-2xl border border-slate-200 space-y-3 shadow-sm h-fit">
          <input type="date" value={form.date} onChange={e => setForm({...form, date: e.target.value})} className="w-full text-xs p-2.5 bg-slate-50 border rounded-xl" />
          <input type="text" placeholder="Ná»™i dung nghiá»‡p vá»¥..." value={form.desc} onChange={e => setForm({...form, desc: e.target.value})} className="w-full text-xs p-2.5 bg-slate-50 border rounded-xl" />
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2">
            <input type="text" placeholder="TK Ná»£" value={form.dr} onChange={e => setForm({...form, dr: e.target.value})} className="w-full text-xs p-2.5 bg-slate-50 border rounded-xl font-mono" />
            <input type="text" placeholder="TK CÃ³" value={form.cr} onChange={e => setForm({...form, cr: e.target.value})} className="w-full text-xs p-2.5 bg-slate-50 border rounded-xl font-mono" />
          </div>
          <input type="number" placeholder="Sá»‘ tiá»n phÃ¡t sinh (VND)..." value={form.amount} onChange={e => setForm({...form, amount: e.target.value})} className="w-full text-xs p-2.5 bg-slate-50 border rounded-xl" />
          <button type="submit" className="w-full bg-emerald-600 text-white font-bold text-xs py-2.5 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center gap-1"><Plus size={14} /> Láº­p Phiáº¿u Ghi Sá»•</button>
        </form>
        <div className="bg-white p-5 rounded-2xl border border-slate-200 col-span-2 shadow-sm overflow-x-auto">
          <table className="w-full text-left text-xs">
            <thead>
              <tr className="bg-slate-50 font-bold border-b"><th className="p-3">NgÃ y</th><th className="p-3">Loáº¡i</th><th className="p-3">Äá»‹nh khoáº£n</th><th className="p-3">Diá»…n giáº£i</th><th className="p-3 text-right">Sá»‘ tiá»n</th><th className="p-3 text-center">HÃ nh Ä‘á»™ng</th></tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody>
              {cashVouchers.map(v => (
                <tr key={v.id} className="border-b">
                  <td className="p-3">{v.voucher_date}</td><td className="p-3 font-bold">{v.voucher_type}</td><td className="p-3 font-mono text-emerald-700">{v.account_dr} / {v.account_cr}</td><td className="p-3">{v.description}</td><td className="p-3 text-right font-bold">{parseFloat(v.amount).toLocaleString()} Ä‘</td>

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { useVouchers } from '../../context/VoucherContext.jsx';
import { BookOpenCheck, RefreshCw } from 'lucide-react';

export default function ClosingProcess() {
  const { vouchers, createNewVoucher } = useVouchers();
  const [log, setLog] = useState('');

  const executeClosing = async () => {
    setLog('Äang bÃ³c tÃ¡ch tá»•ng doanh thu (511) vÃ  giÃ¡ vá»‘n (632)...');
    
    let rev = 0, cogs = 0;
    vouchers.forEach(v => {
      if (v.account_cr === '5111') rev += parseFloat(v.amount);
      if (v.account_dr === '632') cogs += parseFloat(v.amount);
    });

    // PhÃ¡t sinh bÃºt toÃ¡n káº¿t chuyá»ƒn tá»± Ä‘á»™ng
    if (rev > 0) {
      await createNewVoucher({
        voucherDate: '2026-12-31',
        description: 'Káº¿t chuyá»ƒn doanh thu thuáº§n xÃ¡c Ä‘á»‹nh káº¿t quáº£ kinh doanh cuá»‘i ká»³',
        accountDr: '5111', accountCr: '911', amount: rev, type: 'Khac'
      });
    }
    if (cogs > 0) {
      await createNewVoucher({
        voucherDate: '2026-12-31',
        description: 'Káº¿t chuyá»ƒn chi phÃ­ giÃ¡ vá»‘n hÃ ng bÃ¡n cuá»‘i ká»³',
        accountDr: '911', accountCr: '632', amount: cogs, type: 'Khac'
      });
    }

    setLog(`KhÃ³a sá»• thÃ nh cÃ´ng! ÄÃ£ tá»± Ä‘á»™ng sinh bÃºt toÃ¡n káº¿t chuyá»ƒn doanh thu ${rev.toLocaleString()} Ä‘ vÃ  giÃ¡ vá»‘n ${cogs.toLocaleString()} Ä‘ sang tÃ i khoáº£n 911.`);
  };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      <h1 className="text-xl font-black text-slate-800 flex items-center gap-2"><BookOpenCheck className="text-indigo-600" size={24} /> KHÃ“A Sá»” Tá»° Äá»˜NG & Káº¾T CHUYá»‚N KINH DOANH CUá»I Ká»²</h1>
      <div className="bg-white p-6 rounded-2xl border shadow-sm max-w-xl space-y-4">
        <p className="text-xs text-slate-500 leading-relaxed">Há»‡ thá»‘ng quÃ©t toÃ n bá»™ Sá»• cÃ¡i, tá»± Ä‘á»™ng gom sá»‘ dÆ° tÃ i khoáº£n Doanh thu (511), Chi phÃ­ (632, 642) káº¿t chuyá»ƒn tá»± Ä‘á»™ng sang 911 Ä‘á»ƒ xÃ¡c Ä‘á»‹nh Tháº·ng dÆ°/ThÃ¢m há»¥t tÃ i chÃ­nh cá»§a doanh nghiá»‡p phÃ¡p nhÃ¢n.</p>
        <button onClick={executeClosing} className="bg-indigo-600 text-white font-bold text-xs px-4 py-2.5 rounded-xl flex items-center gap-1.5 shadow-md"><RefreshCw size={14} /> Cháº¡y tiáº¿n trÃ¬nh káº¿t chuyá»ƒn khÃ³a sá»•</button>
        {log && <div className="p-4 bg-slate-900 text-emerald-400 font-mono text-xs rounded-xl whitespace-pre-wrap">{log}</div>}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

<file path="front-end/src/views/closing/OpeningBalances.jsx">
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { useAuth } from '../../context/AuthContext.jsx';
import { CHART_OF_ACCOUNTS } from '../../utils/constants.js';
import api from '../../utils/api.js';
import { Coins, Save } from 'lucide-react';

export default function OpeningBalances() {
  const { activeCompany } = useAuth();
  const [balances, setBalances] = useState({});

  useEffect(() => {
    if (activeCompany) loadOpeningBalances();
  }, [activeCompany]);

  const loadOpeningBalances = async () => {
    try {
      const res = await api.get(`/api/opening-balances?company_id=${activeCompany}`);
      const initial = {};
      res.data.forEach(b => {
        initial[b.account_code] = { dr: b.debit_balance, cr: b.credit_balance };
      });
      setBalances(initial);
    } catch (err) { console.error(err); }
  };

  const handleInputChange = (code, field, val) => {
    setBalances({
      ...balances,
      [code]: { ...balances[code], [field]: val }
    });
  };

  const handleSave = async () => {
    try {
      const res = await api.post('/api/opening-balances', { companyId: activeCompany, balances });
      if (res.data.success) alert('LÆ°u sá»‘ dÆ° Ä‘áº§u ká»³ thÃ nh cÃ´ng!');
    } catch { alert('Lá»—i há»‡ thá»‘ng'); }
  };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between border-b pb-4">
        <h1 className="text-xl font-black text-slate-800 flex items-center gap-2"><Coins className="text-amber-500" size={24} /> KHAI BÃO Sá» DÆ¯ Äáº¦U Ká»² Há»† THá»NG TÃ€I KHOáº¢N TT200</h1>
        <button onClick={handleSave} className="bg-emerald-600 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-xl text-xs font-bold flex items-center gap-1.5 shadow-md"><Save size={16} /> LÆ°u báº£ng cÃ¢n Ä‘á»‘i sá»‘ dÆ°</button>
      </div>
      <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border shadow-sm overflow-hidden">
        <table className="w-full text-left text-xs">
          <thead>
            <tr className="bg-slate-50 font-bold border-b"><th className="p-3 w-32">MÃ£ tÃ i khoáº£n</th><th className="p-3">TÃªn tÃ i khoáº£n ThÃ´ng tÆ° 200</th><th className="p-3 text-center">DÆ° Ná»£ Ä‘áº§u ká»³</th><th className="p-3 text-center">DÆ° CÃ³ Ä‘áº§u ká»³</th></tr>
          </thead>
          <tbody className="divide-y">
            {CHART_OF_ACCOUNTS.map(acc => (
              <tr key={acc.code}>
                <td className="p-3 font-mono font-bold text-slate-600">{acc.code}</td>
                <td className="p-3 text-slate-700 font-medium">{acc.name}</td>
                <td className="p-3"><input type="number" placeholder="0" value={balances[acc.code]?.dr || ''} onChange={e => handleInputChange(acc.code, 'dr', e.target.value)} className="w-full p-2 bg-slate-50 border text-xs rounded-lg font-mono text-right" /></td>
                <td className="p-3"><input type="number" placeholder="0" value={balances[acc.code]?.cr || ''} onChange={e => handleInputChange(acc.code, 'cr', e.target.value)} className="w-full p-2 bg-slate-50 border text-xs rounded-lg font-mono text-right" /></td>
              </tr>
            ))}
          </tbody>
        </table>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

<file path="front-end/src/views/costs/WorkInProcess.jsx">
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { useVouchers } from '../../context/VoucherContext.jsx';
import { BookOpenCheck, Layers } from 'lucide-react';

export default function WorkInProcess() {
  const { vouchers, createNewVoucher } = useVouchers();
  const [wipAmount, setWipAmount] = useState('');

  const materialCosts = vouchers.filter(v => v.account_dr === '154').reduce((sum, v) => sum + parseFloat(v.amount), 0);

  const handleProductIn = async () => {
    if (!wipAmount) return;
    await createNewVoucher({
      voucherDate: '2026-06-30',
      description: 'Nháº­p kho thÃ nh pháº©m hoÃ n thÃ nh tá»« xÆ°á»Ÿng sáº£n xuáº¥t dá»Ÿ dang',
      accountDr: '156', accountCr: '154', amount: parseFloat(wipAmount), type: 'Khac'
    });

export default function Payroll() {

  const handleCalculatePayroll = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();

    const base = parseFloat(salary);
    const bhxh = Math.round(base * 0.105); // 10.5% trá»« lÆ°Æ¡ng ngÆ°á»i lao Ä‘á»™ng theo quy Ä‘á»‹nh phÃ¡p luáº­t

    });

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { useVouchers } from '../../context/VoucherContext.jsx';
import { ShoppingBag, Plus } from 'lucide-react';

export default function PurchaseInventory() {
  const { createNewVoucher } = useVouchers();
  const [form, setForm] = useState({ item: '', amount: '', tax: '10' });

  const handlePurchase = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    const baseAmount = parseFloat(form.amount);
    const taxAmount = Math.round(baseAmount * (parseFloat(form.tax) / 100));
    const totalPay = baseAmount + taxAmount;

    // Háº¡ch toÃ¡n tiá»n mua hÃ ng hÃ³a nguyÃªn váº­t liá»‡u nháº­p kho
    await createNewVoucher({
      voucherDate: '2026-01-15',
      description: `Nháº­p kho váº­t tÆ° hÃ ng hÃ³a: ${form.item}`,
      accountDr: '156', accountCr: '331', amount: baseAmount, type: 'Nhap'
    });

    // Háº¡ch toÃ¡n thuáº¿ GTGT Ä‘áº§u vÃ o Ä‘Æ°á»£c kháº¥u trá»«
    if (taxAmount > 0) {
      await createNewVoucher({
        voucherDate: '2026-01-15',
        description: `Thuáº¿ GTGT Ä‘áº§u vÃ o Ä‘Æ°á»£c kháº¥u trá»« cá»§a hÃ³a Ä‘Æ¡n mua hÃ ng ${form.item}`,
        accountDr: '1331', accountCr: '331', amount: taxAmount, type: 'Khac'
      });
    }

    alert(`ÄÃ£ háº¡ch toÃ¡n nháº­p kho hÃ ng hÃ³a. Tá»•ng sá»‘ tiá»n pháº£i tráº£ nhÃ  cung cáº¥p (331): ${totalPay.toLocaleString()} Ä‘`);
    setForm({ item: '', amount: '', tax: '10' });
  };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      <h1 className="text-xl font-black text-slate-800 flex items-center gap-2"><ShoppingBag className="text-emerald-600" size={24} /> PHÃ‚N Há»† MUA HÃ€NG VÃ€ Háº CH TOÃN Váº¬T TÆ¯ NHáº¬P KHO</h1>

        <input type="text" placeholder="TÃªn nguyÃªn váº­t liá»‡u / HÃ ng hÃ³a nháº­p kho..." value={form.item} onChange={e => setForm({...form, item: e.target.value})} className="w-full text-xs p-2.5 bg-slate-50 border rounded-xl" />
        <input type="number" placeholder="GiÃ¡ trá»‹ mua trÆ°á»›c thuáº¿ (VND)..." value={form.amount} onChange={e => setForm({...form, amount: e.target.value})} className="w-full text-xs p-2.5 bg-slate-50 border rounded-xl" />

import React from 'react';
import { useVouchers } from '../../context/VoucherContext.jsx';
import { Percent, Landmark } from 'lucide-react';

export default function TaxReporting() {
  const { vouchers } = useVouchers();

  let vatInput = 0;  // Thuáº¿ GTGT Ä‘áº§u vÃ o Ä‘Æ°á»£c kháº¥u trá»« (1331)
  let vatOutput = 0; // Thuáº¿ GTGT Ä‘áº§u ra pháº£i ná»™p (3331)

  vouchers.forEach(v => {
    if (v.account_dr === '1331') vatInput += parseFloat(v.amount);
    if (v.account_cr === '3331') vatOutput += parseFloat(v.amount);
  });

  const payableVat = vatOutput - vatInput;

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      <h1 className="text-xl font-black text-slate-800 flex items-center gap-2"><Percent className="text-rose-600" size={24} /> Tá»œ KHAI Tá»”NG Há»¢P NGHÄ¨A Vá»¤ THUáº¾ GTGT (MáºªU 01/GTGT)</h1>

          <span className="text-[10px] font-bold text-slate-400 uppercase block">Thuáº¿ GTGT Ä‘áº§u vÃ o tÃ­ch lÅ©y (TK 1331)</span>
          <h3 className="text-lg font-black text-emerald-600">{vatInput.toLocaleString()} Ä‘</h3>
        </div>

          <h3 className="text-lg font-black text-orange-600">{vatOutput.toLocaleString()} Ä‘</h3>

        <div className="bg-white p-5 rounded-2xl border shadow-sm bg-slate-900 text-white">

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { useVouchers } from '../../context/VoucherContext.jsx';
import { Layers, FileSpreadsheet } from 'lucide-react';

export default function AutoSalesExcel() {
  const { createNewVoucher } = useVouchers();
  const [simulatedRows, setSimulatedRows] = useState([]);

  const handleSyncAll = async () => {
    for (const row of simulatedRows) {
      await createNewVoucher({
        voucherDate: '2026-04-01',
        description: `Doanh thu bÃ¡n hÃ ng hÃ³a tá»± Ä‘á»™ng tá»« Excel cho ${row.customer}`,
        accountDr: '131', accountCr: '5111', amount: row.amount, type: 'Xuan'
      });
    }
    alert('ÄÃ£ xá»­ lÃ½ Ä‘á»“ng bá»™ chuá»—i hÃ³a Ä‘Æ¡n Excel vÃ  tá»± Ä‘á»™ng sinh sá»• cÃ¡i háº¡ch toÃ¡n Ná»£ 131 / CÃ³ 5111 thÃ nh cÃ´ng!');
    setSimulatedRows([]);
  };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      <h1 className="text-xl font-black text-slate-800 flex items-center gap-2"><Layers className="text-emerald-600" size={24} /> Äá»’NG Bá»˜ DOANH THU HOÃ ÄÆ N HÃ€NG LOáº T Tá»ª EXCEL</h1>
      <div className="bg-white p-5 rounded-2xl border shadow-sm space-y-4">
        <div className="p-4 border-2 border-dashed border-slate-200 rounded-xl flex flex-col items-center justify-center text-center p-6 bg-slate-50">
          <FileSpreadsheet className="text-emerald-600 mb-2" size={32} />
          <span className="text-xs font-semibold text-slate-600">Há»‡ thá»‘ng sáºµn sÃ ng phÃ¢n tÃ¡ch luá»“ng dá»¯ liá»‡u Excel bÃ¡n ra</span>
        </div>
        {simulatedRows.length > 0 && (
          <div className="space-y-2">
            <button onClick={handleSyncAll} className="bg-emerald-600 text-white font-bold text-xs px-4 py-2 rounded-xl">Äá»“ng bá»™ ghi sá»• toÃ n bá»™ dá»¯ liá»‡u Excel ({simulatedRows.length} hÃ ng)</button>
            <div className="border rounded-xl overflow-hidden text-xs">
              {simulatedRows.map(r => (
                <div key={r.id} className="p-2 border-b flex justify-between bg-white">
                  <span>{r.id} - <b>{r.customer}</b></span>
                  <span className="font-mono font-bold text-slate-700">{r.amount.toLocaleString()} Ä‘</span>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
</file>

<file path="front-end/src/utils/api.js">
import axios from 'axios';

// Giáº£i phÃ¡p thÃ´ng minh: Tá»± Ä‘á»™ng nháº­n diá»‡n mÃ´i trÆ°á»ng lÃ m viá»‡c
let baseURL = import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL;

if (!baseURL) {
  // Náº¿u biáº¿n mÃ´i trÆ°á»ng trá»‘ng vÃ  Ä‘ang cháº¡y thá»±c táº¿ trÃªn mÃ´i trÆ°á»ng web (Railway)
  if (typeof window !== 'undefined' && window.location.hostname !== 'localhost') {
    // Tá»± Ä‘á»™ng láº¥y domain hiá»‡n táº¡i lÃ m gá»‘c cho API (Ãp dá»¥ng khi deploy chung project/monorepo)
    baseURL = window.location.origin; 
  } else {
    // Náº¿u cháº¡y dÆ°á»›i mÃ¡y cÃ¡ nhÃ¢n (Local Development)
    baseURL = 'http://localhost:5000';
  }
}

const api = axios.create({
  baseURL: baseURL
});

// Global request handler: Tá»± Ä‘á»™ng Ä‘Ã­nh kÃ¨m token báº£o máº­t vÃ o Header
api.interceptors.request.use(
  (config) => {
    const token = sessionStorage.getItem('token');
    if (token) {
      config.headers.Authorization = `Bearer ${token}`;
    }
    return config;
  }, 
  (error) => {
    return Promise.reject(error);
  }
);

// Global response handler: Náº¿u phiÃªn lÃ m viá»‡c háº¿t háº¡n (401), dá»n dáº¹p há»‡ thá»‘ng vÃ  Ä‘Ã¡ vá» trang login
api.interceptors.response.use(
  (res) => res,
  (error) => {
    if (error.response?.status === 401) {
      try {
        sessionStorage.removeItem('token');
        sessionStorage.removeItem('user');
        localStorage.removeItem('activeCompany');
      } catch (e) {
        console.error('KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ dá»n dáº¹p bá»™ nhá»› phiÃªn lÃ m viá»‡c:', e);
      }
      
      // Chuyá»ƒn hÆ°á»›ng an toÃ n vá» mÃ n hÃ¬nh Ä‘Äƒng nháº­p gá»‘c
      if (typeof window !== 'undefined' && window.location.pathname !== '/') {
        window.location.href = '/';
      }
    }
    return Promise.reject(error);
  }
);

export default api;

<file path="front-end/src/views/auth/Login.jsx">
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { useAuth } from '../../context/AuthContext.jsx';
import { Lock, User, Terminal } from 'lucide-react';

export default function Login({ onFirstRun }) {
  const { login } = useAuth();
  const [form, setForm] = useState({ username: '', password: '' });
  const [error, setError] = useState('');
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);

  const handleSubmit = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setError('');
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      await login(form.username, form.password);
    } catch (err) {
      setError(err.response?.data?.error || 'KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ káº¿t ná»‘i Ä‘áº¿n mÃ¡y chá»§.');
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-slate-900 p-4">
      <div className="w-full max-w-sm bg-white p-6 rounded-2xl shadow-xl space-y-6">
        <div className="text-center space-y-1">
          <div className="inline-flex p-3 bg-emerald-50 text-emerald-600 rounded-xl mb-2">
            <Terminal size={24} />
          </div>
          <h1 className="text-base font-black text-slate-800 uppercase tracking-wider">Há»‡ thá»‘ng háº¡ch toÃ¡n ERP</h1>
          <p className="text-xs text-slate-400">ÄÄƒng nháº­p tÃ i khoáº£n káº¿ toÃ¡n doanh nghiá»‡p</p>
        </div>

        {error && (
          <div className="p-3 bg-rose-50 border border-rose-100 rounded-xl text-xs font-semibold text-rose-600">
            {error}
          </div>
        )}

        <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-4">
          <div className="space-y-3">
            {/* Ã” nháº­p TÃªn ngÆ°á»i dÃ¹ng - ÄÃ£ thÃªm id, name vÃ  label áº©n */}
            <div className="relative">
              <label htmlFor="username" className="sr-only">TÃªn ngÆ°á»i dÃ¹ng</label>
              <User className="absolute left-3 top-3 text-slate-400" size={16} />
              <input 
                id="username"
                name="username"
                type="text" 
                required 
                disabled={loading}
                placeholder="TÃªn ngÆ°á»i dÃ¹ng..." 
                value={form.username}
                onChange={e => setForm({...form, username: e.target.value})}
                className="w-full text-xs pl-10 pr-4 py-2.5 bg-slate-50 border border-slate-200 rounded-xl focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-emerald-500 disabled:opacity-60" 
              />
            </div>

            {/* Ã” nháº­p Máº­t kháº©u - ÄÃ£ thÃªm id, name vÃ  label áº©n */}
            <div className="relative">
              <label htmlFor="password" className="sr-only">Máº­t kháº©u báº£o máº­t</label>
              <Lock className="absolute left-3 top-3 text-slate-400" size={16} />
              <input 
                id="password"
                name="password"
                type="password" 
                required 
                disabled={loading}
                placeholder="Máº­t kháº©u báº£o máº­t..." 
                value={form.password}
                onChange={e => setForm({...form, password: e.target.value})}
                className="w-full text-xs pl-10 pr-4 py-2.5 bg-slate-50 border border-slate-200 rounded-xl focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-emerald-500 disabled:opacity-60" 
              />
            </div>
          </div>

          <button 
            type="submit" 
            disabled={loading}
            className="w-full bg-slate-900 hover:bg-slate-800 text-white font-bold text-xs py-2.5 rounded-xl shadow-md transition-all disabled:opacity-60"
          >
            {loading ? 'Äang xÃ¡c thá»±c thÃ´ng tin...' : 'XÃ¡c thá»±c & VÃ o há»‡ thá»‘ng'}
          </button>
        </form>

        <div className="border-t border-slate-100 pt-4 text-center">
          <button onClick={onFirstRun} className="text-xs font-bold text-emerald-600 hover:underline">
            ChÆ°a cÃ³ há»‡ thá»‘ng? ÄÄƒng kÃ½ Quáº£n trá»‹ viÃªn khá»Ÿi táº¡o
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

## **ðŸ” Default Admin Account**

Sau khi khá»Ÿi táº¡o database, báº¡n cáº§n táº¡o tÃ i khoáº£n Admin:

1. VÃ o `/api/auth/register-admin` (chá»‰ láº§n Ä‘áº§u):
```bash

  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{"username":"admin","password":"yourpassword"}'
```

2. Hoáº·c INSERT trá»±c tiáº¿p vÃ o database:
